local-id=\"2a5953a5-b35f-4690-8204-d6e65064e4f5\">Intro</h2><ul local-id=\"0fc5258a-4ef6-44a0-af3b-99af9bc84dfd\"><li local-id=\"97c12e68-ba6b-44f6-bad3-1b3db5799200\"><p projected utilisation of Pro benefitsâ€‹</p></li><li local-id=\"cbcc3989-6834-4eae-9c98-42fa59fbcb39\"><p local-id=\"99c5ff57-3025-48da-9a55-ee9687c5cbfe\">Based on this analysis, <strong>28% of Plus <strong>strengthen retention</strong></p></li></ul><h2 local-id=\"cd926645-eb39-458a-8c6f-80f3cabe0cf3\">Reflections from Plus</h2><table data-table-width=\"1170\" data-layout=\"center\" ac:local-id=\"a886577b-ff44-41aa-aa87-38e7b6537d71\"><p local-id=\"ceff72e3-a36a-40c4-b912-82a51fadef5d\"><ac:inline-comment-marker ac:ref=\"0f4a390b-dda2-49cc-b92e-83700dafee01\">At rollout, launch one primary cohort where customers are released at the same time -&gt; analyse power users as a subset, not a separate cohort.</ac:inline-comment-marker></p></td></tr><tr ac:local-id=\"f23ae622-5766-4876-a2a0-ab92c22b9664\"><td ac:local-id=\"63aa7b7e-c37b-4aeb-b01f-ad7685747e47\"><p local-id=\"1d6486f7-7f8a-4854-9946-662c8f1b89fe\">Experiment Data</p></td><td ac:local-id=\"c1c87da8-e4b2-43ee-875d-cdea70fc668b\"><p local-id=\"ac03586a-da79-434a-b948-da57c4b29ceb\"><ac:inline-comment-marker ac:ref=\"aa90b73a-cc4e-4e0f-af51-2eb249bd0ac7\">MVP 1 control and treatment groups were not statistically identical.</ac:inline-comment-marker></p></td><td ac:local-id=\"8492a730-cc21-4a42-ba1a-1202806da7fc\"><p groups are statistically identical before launch. </p></td></tr><tr ac:local-id=\"6e1205c3-a839-4a45-8d34-877479a9a197\"><td ac:local-id=\"f10bf793-94a4-4576-90bc-fcbebe0dddc8\"><p groups' start date  was not equal to the true start date due to batch updating - this was as a result of 1% launchdarkly rollout.</p></td><td ac:local-id=\"aa2460f8-c381-477e-b59b-e5301aef7293\"><p over time.</p></td><td ac:local-id=\"32dfe9ea-0b38-4f0d-990c-46d8afd78724\"><p local-id=\"8fd1ff6a-a930-4c49-914f-9224d50841cb\"><ac:inline-comment-marker ac:ref=\"82667ce3-84e6-4ffb-8caf-e60723b1a3f5\">Avoid 1% LaunchDarkly rollouts for experiments; assign customers explicitly from a defined list</ac:inline-comment-marker></p></td></tr><tr ac:local-id=\"3871fd8d-1d49-4db8-b851-f2bd3cdf2fce\"><td ac:local-id=\"2d4d9f54-c194-43c3-80db-68a61e56d71e\"><p local-id=\"7577125f-94d3-46c8-ac19-732974b9c101\">Experiment Data</p></td><td ac:local-id=\"bf03d2cb-b810-459d-8757-d09b6631425e\"><p local-id=\"5da6d663-20fa-4bc1-8ef9-621de8cb8f3b\">Lots of cohorts were repeats of each other.</p></td><td ac:local-id=\"2fe4d20c-3fd9-4f5f-8cee-d30d7b16846f\"><p local-id=\"5d1aae6b-b658-4a83-bc91-6e52a969aa9e\">Added complexity to the number of cohorts - no one was clear on which cohorts were which.</p></td><td ac:local-id=\"6fe4753e-b939-41e8-9be5-48a74fc27bad\"><p local-id=\"577d65d9-2a09-47ee-89bc-5068653b462c\"><ac:inline-comment-marker ac:ref=\"810161ac-a743-41f8-90bf-5a06cb3d8ce0\">Only create new cohorts when they differ meaningfully in theme or eligibility criteria.</ac:inline-comment-marker></p></td></tr><tr ac:local-id=\"9745c1eb-bf0b-432e-9183-ea72bd7b77db\"><td ac:local-id=\"40613690-0d77-42e7-bf9e-8d55e6445e83\"><p local-id=\"90ebdb3b-2a0f-4308-b363-0701c9a8c0dc\">Experiment Data</p></td><td ac:local-id=\"1129b0c1-1996-48e1-addb-6a6fad54859a\"><p local-id=\"17302358-8f7e-43ea-bc2e-296d07e46542\">Unnecessary complexity</p></td><td ac:local-id=\"5a94a3b5-7f1d-465c-b8b1-84d333842ea3\"><p ac:local-id=\"198e320a-889d-48c9-8a6c-8735f1d288bb\"><td ac:local-id=\"5985fd6b-9661-4d53-b8d5-c2ad0efd739e\"><p local-id=\"93dc982f-5c23-4385-b50e-0c01d3b3ffab\">Cohort Rollouts</p></td><td ac:local-id=\"84ba9be6-7d1b-43e9-b40b-716fdceb4b2d\"><p local-id=\"c453eb9e-b776-4b34-a1b6-77d6dd7d0120\">Duplication and lack of clarity on measuring eligibility</p></td><td ac:local-id=\"800105c3-53c2-45af-a0e1-34e7e96989ff\"><ul local-id=\"24680af2-e6e3-4cf1-b54b-1f44fdfb4b9a\"><li local-id=\"66f1033c-b5ae-4ae5-8ce7-7d91fa94153d\"><p local-id=\"2ff78d09-c290-4887-9346-f8b7784060df\">One person is in at most one treatment group</p></li><li local-id=\"5d90f81c-1266-4069-99ea-596602eb5d9e\"><p local-id=\"578853ea-4b65-4436-996a-69f9ac4ac4d0\">Each person who is eligible for pro should be in a treatment group</p></li></ul></td></tr><tr ac:local-id=\"c846571d-2430-41d0-b487-18369fe04a53\"><td ac:local-id=\"2f699b51-f99d-4797-bf6a-62109b26a0ef\"><p local-id=\"b812ad0a-948b-4d59-a258-acabfea3980c\">Communication</p></td><td ac:local-id=\"fd2f8e18-0670-4f0b-a064-3cf5884866e5\"><p released, and the rollout log was not strictly maintained.</ac:inline-comment-marker></p></td><td ac:local-id=\"900aa365-e74a-45b4-a3ca-a075f2036670\"><p ac:local-id=\"adeb7622-69d9-4a05-84e8-90926780d28a\"><ul local-id=\"90b23d2f-2767-4397-aabc-12fd98d4c970\"><li local-id=\"4e1222a8-f6cc-41ee-9769-428ca5dd5ab7\"><p local-id=\"2c3b43f4-d6f4-41d2-992f-920daccac76a\">Inform relevant stakeholders that a cohort has gone live</p></li><li local-id=\"f3b85d7a-acce-4636-bc43-0e0fb7606f3c\"><p local-id=\"11520f08-86ad-417f-9691-d2204b839d03\">Keep log up to date and user friendly.</p></li></ul></td></tr><tr ac:local-id=\"b293aca7-3276-40fb-815d-c0ec6f9b648c\"><td ac:local-id=\"2d24a543-acb0-48f5-83c4-648e6a7236d9\"><p local-id=\"c7bdaefe-659d-46af-954f-5d1e3d51d232\">Data Preparedness</p></td><td ac:local-id=\"6785b5e8-a930-45e1-bd4d-6b181bbdcdfa\"><p local-id=\"9480e543-83ed-4d09-b6fd-a7f4315c5351\">Rewards logic wasn&rsquo;t built into the PnL at launch.</p></td><td ac:local-id=\"c153e3c3-7206-4373-b23c-eca221a46931\"><p Profit</ac:inline-comment-marker></p></td><td ac:local-id=\"14c86f92-d321-42ff-be7f-280488afa950\"><p local-id=\"18d9f7d5-155d-4a78-993b-5d2b353c270e\">Ensure the reward logic for Pro is built into the PnL.</p></td></tr></tbody></table><h2 local-id=\"2ff6e62b-ff73-4108-a869-a9e27b25e69a\">Key Questions</h2><ul local-id=\"24cc960f-2ef7-4326-ae48-f0f6c7dc4dde\"><li local-id=\"36059805-2c26-4301-9c64-eaf129cee209\"><p local-id=\"1a2ebc90-30f0-408f-a416-a8308251b864\">Lifecycle</p><ul local-id=\"c2899064-f8db-40ac-98c8-f1456a8dbd15\"><li local-id=\"7187f232-a5c2-4275-ab76-99cfd63bd519\"><p local-id=\"a02f98f9-583e-4e00-8b8e-2f919e080238\">Will the top 20-30% of Plus Customers adopt Pro as predicted?</p></li><li local-id=\"04f51be0-977d-4a74-904a-f128684c8598\"><p local-id=\"e09ca798-803e-4db1-8a5b-5ba5e1b743be\">How many people who didnt adopt Plus, adopt Pro?</p></li><li local-id=\"d2f380f0-8707-4497-9aaa-89d2dc1f41b5\"><p local-id=\"8f373a56-ea32-4cbc-819c-ce8d2d07d90c\">Will Pro users retain at the same rate as Plus?</p></li><li local-id=\"4c2fe132-d572-411d-8703-75f378278fa7\"><p local-id=\"4504a0ea-e5c1-4516-a104-35e9bf7708d3\">Are they using the Pro benefits?</p><ul local-id=\"c43cf775-da49-402f-963d-fbe999e0a9f3\"><li local-id=\"60b0685a-2eab-403d-801d-6ff6b4af7798\"><p local-id=\"85828101-0568-4849-b3c6-505e814bc12d\">Free snoozes</p></li><li local-id=\"63746ac8-b013-4278-83da-c49b29168d77\"><p local-id=\"92309b5d-2e09-43ab-b34c-e60e520a3a32\">Extra 1% on debit ecj spend</p></li><li local-id=\"c60e9130-4942-4879-bae7-946011bcca95\"><p local-id=\"327fe1b7-fb92-4f4f-a585-c55d5511e1b9\">Other</p></li></ul></li></ul></li><li local-id=\"fc1407f5-1b96-485c-b0d8-2b7b1a85326e\"><p local-id=\"b3dec3b7-924a-4ee5-9dfe-efd04e4cc9b4\">Financial</p><ul local-id=\"3d7e1869-3c04-40cf-8623-f4c1a080995b\"><li local-id=\"826d3996-8829-451e-9880-23218db71ede\"><p local-id=\"2315e1d0-c9dc-4451-ac7b-3210e77ea930\">Will Pro users increase/change their spend with us? (GMV, credit, and unlock mix)?</p></li><li local-id=\"fc4157e8-dce3-4add-b483-ed7d95f1d465\"><p local-id=\"dcf8ded6-2a11-44bc-acc6-fdfde643a9c4\">Will Pro users become more profitable than they were in Plus?</p></li></ul></li></ul><h2 local-id=\"4edb2e3a-0dfd-4b94-a8bf-c65ed91cbbf0\">Technical Discovery</h2><p local-id=\"736dc6f0-b187-4b3a-8150-9755ea4f4a04\">With the new targeting service, we can give Engineering a list of customers we want to offer Pro to with minimal restrictions. This means:</p><ul local-id=\"968d143a-cfb7-4bff-91d2-dbe3caf0201e\"><li local-id=\"351817e7-10e3-4ce9-9c39-dd29b25a86d9\"><p local-id=\"6b5dbf75-009d-40a4-990c-0e4f6a656ae0\">We can choose it to be as big as we want (100k would take ITAM a few hours to upload but wouldn't be a problem )</p></li><li local-id=\"fd4f9e67-6a4a-4cc1-9f36-705f865d972a\"><p local-id=\"ff9e4211-36b8-4981-9dc4-5388ba78ff30\">We can ensure our treatment and control are statistically comparable before handing it over</p></li></ul><p local-id=\"6f70707b-e402-4f98-8da7-a009458cf194\">The only potential blocker that was raised is ensuring that customers have been offered plus previously, which should be everyone by the time Zilch Pro is ready for launch. If this is not the case,  it's possible from a targeting and back-end point of view, but the front end wouldn't be accommodated for this scenario. We can ensure that customers in our treatment group meet the eligibility condition of plus.&nbsp;</p><h1 local-id=\"d1d41b93-ce8a-4342-b1d4-20611069d39f\">Ideal Experiment Design</h1><h2 local-id=\"29ad6842-a2aa-489f-9071-40b2fa09d23d\">Customer Selection</h2><p local-id=\"c5207c04-2323-4cd5-8201-64d5b05f04ba\">Ideally, we draw a subset of MAUs as illustrated in the below diagram. This would ensure we can answer all key lifecycle questions.</p><ac:image ac:align=\"center\" ac:layout=\"center\" ac:original-height=\"849\" ac:original-width=\"1614\" ac:custom-width=\"true\" ac:local-id=\"b851c7fa-6719-4875-980c-9a4615565b46\" ac:alt=\"image-20260113-141351.png\" ac:width=\"760\"><ri:attachment ri:filename=\"image-20260113-141351.png\" ri:version-at-save=\"1\" /></ac:image><p local-id=\"ad690aab-be63-432d-ac4f-3281ab8dcc2a\">What needs to be determined, though, is whether we could use a sample big enough to draw statistically significant findings on our key metric (GMV per User) while answering those lifecycle questions.</p><h2 local-id=\"145affdb-c057-4a0e-8d7c-4e6422028584\">Metrics </h2><p local-id=\"19cbf66c-8b5d-4ca4-a83e-e0c711612ace\">Key</p><ul local-id=\"e45d52f2-ad6a-4bc6-9b92-8b55f2ffddd0\"><li local-id=\"78f62197-d8fc-44c5-a3cf-8ef7e14fe089\"><p local-id=\"11c234e5-23f3-41b7-9952-3e87f6055aa5\">GP per User</p></li><li local-id=\"90e87fc8-e342-41e0-b7d1-1db09583dec2\"><p local-id=\"826843a9-dabc-478f-92db-f0befdc16fce\">Penetration of</p><ul local-id=\"261ffe52-a6d5-48f0-9a1a-122fa604e707\"><li local-id=\"d354c696-41a2-4ca0-ad44-dfa52b122eed\"><p local-id=\"3ee3d226-1342-4eae-b859-7c914a4d2a65\">Plus MAUs</p></li><li local-id=\"554f8d6b-d6b1-4c03-aaab-bef7520daa09\"><p local-id=\"5f09e765-ce0f-4a3d-affe-ceabd05360c9\">MAUs who demonstrated PMF</p></li><li local-id=\"46c46507-e7f3-4bab-83ac-e7e53481aa16\"><p local-id=\"0f70f94b-85a4-413a-a4a4-16613b5fa8b6\">Total MAUs</p></li></ul></li></ul><p local-id=\"22c357c0-40b2-4a08-a2fd-352d9869017b\">Other</p><p local-id=\"bfec31f1-0b4d-49b5-92c8-d160c0dc2773\">Lifecycle</p><ul local-id=\"a6cd63ab-29ea-40f7-a1a9-cc99c2fb310b\"><li local-id=\"c7143dec-8bde-4083-9463-e6f0a0fb27d4\"><p local-id=\"f585b544-1b7b-4be0-8c8a-ea510476ad9f\">Adoption and Retention of MAUs/Plus MAUs/ PMF MAUs</p></li><li local-id=\"abec53ad-c264-417c-b65c-0ebaeb761e2b\"><p local-id=\"de73f8c7-8c67-4c90-ac23-8f24785a061e\">Utilisation of benefits</p></li><li local-id=\"d8527b6a-f72d-4b35-a44e-aadcb4650dc9\"><p local-id=\"29e024f7-e067-48f6-b297-44d7bd293f23\">Customer retention (Longer term)</p></li></ul><p local-id=\"f324635d-bd6c-4c4c-9f9a-d7e590a68c66\">Financial</p><ul local-id=\"07109ede-a9d3-487b-8e2b-c914c8f186e9\"><li local-id=\"d6cabe18-3101-4e34-a5ae-bc19ef0de365\"><p local-id=\"f5591029-7098-4bb1-a2ba-28de74857663\">GMV per User</p></li><li local-id=\"e251a429-664d-4d64-a36d-49aff9a25671\"><p local-id=\"5d3cc3bd-52d6-4a93-aa37-79684c6d2b04\">GP lift on customers who were GP negative on Plus</p></li><li local-id=\"a44129f7-ec81-4167-b8bc-42f242e72628\"><p local-id=\"aba112a4-73b3-4c4d-b364-85cfc24b5f07\">Credit/ Debit split</p></li><li local-id=\"79830dee-24f9-48fe-9c13-7c5d9bded00c\"><p local-id=\"933e9536-5bd6-4842-a414-a81a7421c94a\">Anywhere/ECJ/Express split</p></li></ul><h2 local-id=\"8077a95d-d3a9-4b5b-8342-518ac7f67187\">Power Analysis</h2><h3 local-id=\"bce19e2e-ad5a-43b9-8928-fdc9af4b8406\">Subset of MAUs</h3><p local-id=\"3671e645-b726-4419-bd5d-3392bc4745d9\">Using GMV per User as a primary metric we want to increase (same as <ac:link><ri:page ri:content-title=\"Memberships MVP experiment plan\" ri:version-at-save=\"104\" /><ac:link-body>MVP Experimentation plan</ac:link-body></ac:link>), I will conduct a power analysis assuming 3% adoption of people offered.</p><ul local-id=\"160ecf31-c977-47d3-8ffc-6484a2d09f80\"><li local-id=\"635bb750-9a8f-4a66-8f6b-0b87fe5cbb8f\">0.14</p></td><td ac:local-id=\"9774c2ef-7a79-42f4-9490-737ae956164c\"><p local-id=\"4203664a-e0c6-4bfb-95c3-ba7ab0425e15\">796.949928</p></td><td ac:local-id=\"cfcf3a7b-6f36-4d9f-b10a-fabb2957b362\"><p local-id=\"95f82132-219b-4376-b143-239b18788b3b\">0.25</p></td><td ac:local-id=\"9e0d6153-10e5-4f90-9101-2f80cefb2edf\"><p local-id=\"5c9f3f49-f9e4-4117-91e6-debe21da3be0\">27.8932475</p></td><td ac:local-id=\"13b7ca44-4b9a-4a31-afda-7e4e72086d59\"><p local-id=\"b8e8f407-6613-4fd9-b51e-b8ff22027c19\">7726</p></td></tr></tbody></table><ac:structured-macro ac:name=\"info\" ac:schema-version=\"1\" ac:local-id=\"0604f292-dc96-4e4c-a426-770fb78341e1\" ac:macro-id=\"2a7190a5-9f04-45d8-adbc-3ef6a3e9daff\"><ac:rich-text-body><p local-id=\"7bb6323c-6e3c-499c-8744-afcac0359d12\">With a 10k sample size, 5% alpha and 80% power, we would be able to detect a +12% lift in GMV amongst adopters. This would present as a +3% lift in GMV in the treatment v control groups.</p></ac:rich-text-body></ac:structured-macro><h1 local-id=\"5e025e6c-adbd-470b-aae6-5c4a98b7e5c7\">Actual Experiment Design</h1><h2 local-id=\"48113546-d40e-43db-8eee-15836e197174\">Customer Selection</h2><ac:structured-macro ac:name=\"tip\" ac:schema-version=\"1\" ac:local-id=\"5206cd98-e72d-43ed-872d-6fae94ef2b69\" ac:macro-id=\"b4018f47-96c2-4f27-aab6-e35f897adb24\"><ac:rich-text-body><p local-id=\"6414938a-302d-4e1c-a858-c69e69860744\">Despite reflecting on the complexity of having two experiment groups for the MVP launch, it is clear that using a subset of MAUs for Pro will not be sufficient to draw any learnings on the financial side. Therefore, it will make sense to take two approaches: 1 subset of MAUs for lifecycle learnings, and 1 subset of Plus MAUs for financial learnings.</p></ac:rich-text-body></ac:structured-macro><ac:image ac:align=\"center\" ac:layout=\"center\" ac:original-height=\"849\" ac:original-width=\"1614\" ac:custom-width=\"true\" local-id=\"9570573b-d12a-4911-8586-5348563c8f5a\">Technical Rollout</h2><p local-id=\"1daebd25-90c9-4919-812c-828bec52a5db\">With the new targeting service, the data team would be able to create four lists of customers:</p><ul local-id=\"78fcf093-0aa9-40b3-b366-edf535fbd3f5\"><li local-id=\"5b2f38e9-16c6-4456-a582-6329459a0457\"><p local-id=\"b2ba295f-4030-4067-a340-b9111a2266ad\">Treatment 1 (MAUs) - Business Decision</p></li><li local-id=\"6600f4e7-8f0e-4091-bbae-62a473338107\"><p local-id=\"ca338c67-e185-4755-8906-309a255eda89\">Control 1 (MAUs)</p></li><li local-id=\"c2d376ad-1874-449d-b91d-14b2f7ba4252\"><p local-id=\"831cfe26-9a23-4120-afc4-571eed06ea99\">Treatment 2 (Plus MAUs) - 10k</p></li><li local-id=\"be11c4f2-68ea-45ae-9744-8965f3ff4ac6\"><p added to the targetting service at the same time. We would also tag the customers appropriately in mrt experiment and ensure no overlap.</p><p local-id=\"ccc38cb3-1078-40f2-b675-071b9d787d56\">Next steps</p><ul local-id=\"8bdbef08-3dc7-4cae-8f27-9169b8d8f05c\"><li local-id=\"ae33134b-284b-4c52-a455-634c56d0273a\"><p local-id=\"70e98209-1f12-46fd-9775-a132c6c8e510\">GTM plan</p></li><li local-id=\"35d23b4b-dfbe-4f03-bb8b-1d316ba17aaf\"><p local-id=\"2bd18f90-34b4-4184-a4aa-71e755134b5b\">Roll out plan timeline</p></li></ul><p local-id=\"74d3e3a2-4fe6-4a58-88a1-fe6df6d2eea0\" />"}}

Paid Plus Remaining Days &rarr; converted into Pro Days which is ~10 days</p><ul local-id=\"c5a8c4e5-a2ed-4dbd-a947-4f4174505bfb\"><li local-id=\"826caeac-ebfb-46ac-8e9f-62a865115ae4\"><p local-id=\"84977b3e-9bf5-4c6d-9473-3171ab5010ec\">&pound;3.99 (plus) / Current Month (31 for this example) = &pound;0.1287096774</p></li><li local-id=\"234d6395-e2b1-4d98-b236-10449f851b59\"><p local-id=\"5498f21e-b2fc-4777-a2bb-aeb25ea8f820\">&pound;0.1287096774 * 21 days (remaining of this billing cycle) = &pound;2.7029032254</p></li><li local-id=\"eb0f2023-ee26-447d-8d52-8668c005ec60\"><p local-id=\"bf368ee2-5087-425a-a4cc-e031d5b3bdee\">&pound;7.99 (pro) / Current Month (31 for this example) = &pound;0.2577419355</p></li><li local-id=\"68ade42d-28eb-475a-8585-96ad92c59ddf\"><p local-id=\"6df47ab0-4196-43e7-9174-5b8512ec37bd\">&pound;2.7029032254 / &pound;0.2577419355 = 10.486</p></li></ul><p local-id=\"45ed7e88-edaa-4082-871d-21dd56e7888f\">So Next Billing Date should be ~ 21st January 2026, where they will be charged the full Pro Fee</p></ac:rich-text-body></ac:structured-macro></td></tr><tr ac:local-id=\"53a989f2-3561-41de-8563-b649aefc67fa\"><td ac:local-id=\"c040917a-1d86-4c08-b435-09541be2a5d0\"><p local-id=\"3fb0742c-27d7-478b-a729-cb96d6890352\">Plus (free trial) &rarr; Pro</p></td><td ac:local-id=\"f9d09454-c3eb-43ff-b6b7-cf5dd0f52afd\"><p local-id=\"70dc44c7-d49b-4540-883a-de7707dac43d\"><strong>Remaining days of Plus free trial are converted into Pro free trial days</strong></p><p local-id=\"ec9d1406-dcc9-4945-9ce1-c626d503d08e\">Same calculation as above</p><ul local-id=\"3e893297-bdf9-446f-8ac0-07253176bbd6\"><li </p><ul local-id=\"9bbc8a6b-d19c-4949-89d1-d1719b6e446e\"><li local-id=\"a5ac2960-8731-4d01-a0dc-0b0fe20307a0\"><p local-id=\"462fe857-7928-4fba-aa7c-d3abaf290ed6\">Renewal date = <time **Zilch AI**

memberships</p></li></ul></td></tr></tbody></table><h2 local-id=\"cf9aef06851c\">Features to Paywall Behind Memberships</h2><p local-id=\"eea9176795af\">The following lists outline the features currently available to Standard members. Standard member benefits represent features that could be gated behind a membership with low to medium business risk. Core business benefits represent features that could be gated behind a membership but carry higher business risk due to their impact on the core value proposition.</p></ac:layout-cell></ac:layout-section><ac:layout-section ac:type=\"two_equal\" ac:breakout-mode=\"wide\" ac:breakout-width=\"760\" ac:local-id=\"c83c44936b02\"><ac:layout-cell ac:local-id=\"b5f968724499\"><p local-id=\"758c5b49e5e6\"><strong>Standard Member Benefits</strong></p><ul local-id=\"5aa190223701\"><li local-id=\"d0fc54deb565\"><p local-id=\"a4a25dc098fb\">Foreign Exchange</p></li><li local-id=\"318e4e291971\"><p local-id=\"48143be2d72b\">No debit Rewards on Express</p></li><li local-id=\"14a92fcb79c6\"><p local-id=\"a508d7b520e5\">Zilch Travel</p></li><li local-id=\"c032f7d89a17\"><p local-id=\"a16dd5dde8c9\">Gift cards</p></li><li local-id=\"a72bc4be4082\"><p local-id=\"5602cde9f1ba\">Vouchers</p></li><li local-id=\"65d9102f85f9\"><p local-id=\"005c3c26ffda\">Zilch Compare</p></li><li local-id=\"d9be291c3614\"><p local-id=\"0f25003ef43a\">Multiple debit cards</p></li><li local-id=\"1a195f53efc5\"><p local-id=\"115e3bd2e5ad\">Delay Rewards</p></li><li local-id=\"6755b2f84bf6\"><p local-id=\"133d0b711df8\">Spending Rewards</p></li><li local-id=\"8e83b97b97b6\"><p local-id=\"ff45f559d9ca\">App icon personalisation</p></li><li **Zilch AI**
{"type":"tool_call","tool_call":{"id":"tooluse_yemf9h1dM0jaAAhb4kGtU5","name":"confluence_page_mcp_Atlassian","args":"{\"pageId\":\"4899143704\"}","type":"tool_call","progress":1,"output":"**Memberships Strategy**\nID: 4899143704\nURL: https://payzilch.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/ZP/pages/4899143704/Memberships+Strategy\nSpace: Zilch Product\nLabels: \nType: page\nCreated: 2025-12-12T10:37:22.664Z\nLast Modified: 2025-12-15T15:05:41.361Z\n\n<ac:layout><ac:layout-section ac:type=\"fixed-width\" ac:breakout-mode=\"default\"><ac:layout-cell><p local-id=\"b7ad770f-a871-44ae-a5ce-f8d137574913\"><strong>Table of Contents</strong></p><ac:structured-macro ac:name=\"toc\" ac:schema-version=\"1\" data-layout=\"default\" ac:local-id=\"9ef99580-fc8e-4a26-86c6-04cda5e5d6f7\" ac:macro-id=\"a5916990-abe6-4f82-ab32-c8542b5b712d\"><ac:parameter ac:name=\"style\">none</ac:parameter></ac:structured-macro><h2 local-id=\"328d5c63-dd08-449d-a8ea-cb36cede53e3\">Executive Summary</h2><p local-id=\"d9c49302-d94e-4356-aa5f-457b63dfea3e\">The launch of Zilch Plus has demonstrated that memberships are a powerful lever for growth at Zilch, driving incremental GP per customer, establishing a recurring revenue stream, and showing early signals of improved retention. While the current membership model provides a clear value ladder from free to premium, organic adoption of Plus and Pro alone is projected to reach only ~17% paid MAU penetration by March 2027. Given the strong early performance of Plus and clear customer appetite for paid value, there is an opportunity to accelerate adoption and scale memberships further, with an ambition to reach 100k paid MAUs over the same timeframe.</p><p local-id=\"fc617b4c-17f8-4443-9921-b4c6672e53bf\">This strategy sets out how memberships can evolve into a core, scalable engine for long-term growth and profitability, informed by early learnings from Zilch Plus in market, a deep understanding of our customers, and insights generated through a cross-functional strategy workshop. Grounded in the role memberships play in customers&rsquo; everyday financial lives, the strategy focuses on delivering increasing value as engagement deepens - elevating everyday value, enhancing lifestyle, rewarding meaningful behaviours, and giving customers greater control and confidence over their money. By addressing gaps in the current tier structure and reworking Rewards into a more sustainable points-based model, the strategy creates a clear, scalable framework to grow paid adoption, deepen engagement, improve GP margin, and align customer value with long-term, sustainable business outcomes.</p><h2 local-id=\"83778729-f05c-4dfb-9c9f-8bb7bcfc7cb5\">Membership Strategy Current State</h2><p local-id=\"22e53732-a8f4-4ec0-8b18-1156284bbb6a\">The current membership model provides a clear and progressive value ladder, rewarding customers with increasing benefits as their engagement grows and incentivising higher frequency and share of spend with Zilch.</p><ac:image ac:align=\"center\" ac:layout=\"center\" ac:original-height=\"588\" ac:original-width=\"1232\" ac:custom-width=\"true\" ac:local-id=\"032827ff-1a4f-428f-9913-02b29b356903\" ac:alt=\"image-20251214-151734.png\" ac:width=\"760\"><ri:attachment ri:filename=\"image-20251214-151734.png\" ri:version-at-save=\"1\" /></ac:image><h3 local-id=\"258b099f-7fa7-4430-babd-c9da7370c371\"><strong>Zilch Standard</strong></h3><p local-id=\"ecc7a5e3-b75b-43ee-bf2d-67c60bf743e1\">Zilch Standard is Zilch&rsquo;s free membership proposition, providing access to affordable credit through fees subsidised by ASPIN, alongside a Rewards offering on debit purchases. It is designed for customers who want low-cost credit and simple rewards when they spend. Strategically, Standard acts as the entry point to the Zilch ecosystem, with the primary objective of increasing credit utilisation and growing share of wallet.</p><h3 local-id=\"0518a54d-ff9f-4ce8-8fda-436dd9e7f91d\"><strong>Zilch Plus</strong></h3><p local-id=\"8b38c6bf-d66e-4051-a9d6-39857a38698d\">Zilch Plus is the first paid tier in Zilch&rsquo;s memberships portfolio. Soft-launched in July 2025 and rolling out to all customers by January 2026, Plus is priced at &pound;3.99 per month and offers clear, tangible value through enhanced Rewards, complemented by lifestyle benefits such as Tastecard. Plus is aimed at customers who want to get more value back from their everyday spending. Once customers reach this tier, the strategic focus is to increase spend with Zilch, strengthen retention, and grow ARPU.</p><h3 local-id=\"6afd52a2-e011-442f-94da-560d79b626b4\"><strong>Zilch Pro</strong></h3><p local-id=\"b44e6061-52b8-4259-aa82-5a5d4030b58b\">Zilch Pro is planned to launch in March 2026 as a premium tier positioned above Plus, priced at &pound;7.99 per month. Pro delivers primarily intangible value through partnerships and enhanced credit features such as free Snoozes, alongside incremental tangible value through Rewards on debit purchases. It is targeted at Zilch&rsquo;s most highly engaged customers, expected to represent approximately 30% of the top Plus cohort. The strategic objective of Pro is to make Zilch the primary spend card for these customers while improving GP margin by migrating high-engagement Plus users into a higher-value tier. In addition, the introduction of Pro creates a clear value anchor that enhances the perceived value of Plus, helping to drive incremental membership adoption from Standard customers.</p><h2 local-id=\"2b1b524a-6eda-4a03-9c54-da07245011e0\"><strong>Taking Memberships to the Next Level</strong></h2><p local-id=\"2297d2a6-f314-436a-8166-d4ad3132b407\">While our current membership strategy has been effective, we are projected to reach approximately 17% paid penetration of MAUs by March 2027 through organic adoption of Plus and Pro alone. Given the strong early signals from Plus in market, there is an opportunity to accelerate adoption and outperform this trajectory. <strong>Our ambition is to reach 100k paid MAUs within the same timeframe, which will require an evolution of the current strategy</strong> to unlock broader and faster membership uptake.</p><blockquote local-id=\"c79ddcc3-053a-4ca1-bf6d-dda9d7905b38\"><p local-id=\"4b25f6da-7a01-4c6b-9c9c-d888ae844e14\"><em>How might we build a compelling loyalty offering to grow our paid member base to 100k by March 2027?&rdquo;</em></p></blockquote><h2 local-id=\"ecae9fc3-55af-46b0-8c21-7446bbcb8225\">Memberships Strategy Workshop</h2><p local-id=\"22a4423d-c8db-4d2d-94a7-bd1cd5f2319e\">As a cross-functional memberships working group, we came together for a structured workshop session to define how we deliver against our HMW statement. The session focused on two core outcomes:</p><p local-id=\"80886d27-a721-4bb9-ad81-a3babdbbd734\"><strong>First</strong>, to define a clear vision for memberships by identifying who memberships are for, the role they play within the Zilch ecosystem, and the outcomes this vision should deliver for the business. This vision will act as a guiding north star for all future membership decisions.</p><p local-id=\"07c5e8ea-0ebd-4cb4-a6b9-222638a43db9\"><strong>Second</strong>, to identify the key strategic opportunities required to realise this vision, forming the foundation of the 2026&ndash;2027 memberships roadmap.</p><h2 local-id=\"0940ffb2-9fdb-4f3f-b029-b8114267fef7\">Vision Statement Outcomes</h2><p local-id=\"344881ef-a5e0-473f-9194-0674a1aa4291\">During the workshop, we worked in groups to generate the following insights, which informed the development of our memberships vision:</p><p local-id=\"741e7a03-1485-41d0-86e4-a09778cdcd54\"><strong>Who did we identify as our customers?</strong></p><ul local-id=\"8f0159f4-4591-4a20-b0bf-ff816be65d8c\"><li local-id=\"3cd2c3db-ad5a-46b4-bd87-3e8b3b526f49\"><p local-id=\"f52717e3-4289-4ee3-8663-c35de1f8df7c\">Value-driven everyday spenders</p></li><li local-id=\"ea348db5-a4ab-4d39-9d2e-6ef9ab2d1a21\"><p local-id=\"3ccfdd98-d47f-4bfd-bf36-99d3c6bc727f\">Credit-reliant customers seeking control</p></li><li local-id=\"c760bc90-809f-47ef-ab94-388a75652960\"><p local-id=\"1297903e-53f2-4e5b-a285-4bbba1a6fd87\">Engaged Zilch loyalists</p></li><li local-id=\"bf9a7ca3-4bb5-44a4-8846-33c72f42bf3b\"><p local-id=\"4c4ae411-3428-491e-afae-8984f2d30508\">High-spend optimisers</p></li><li local-id=\"235ca8e8-83d3-4d67-86be-33f3b79a066d\"><p local-id=\"96152b99-538f-49fd-9154-1b082d8e782e\">&ldquo;Smart money&rdquo; users motivated by rewards and recognition</p></li></ul><p local-id=\"ab6e2c30-851e-49b5-ae82-5680c1cf80e5\"><strong>What value and purpose can we offer these customers?</strong></p><ul local-id=\"8910159e-2d50-4d06-b8d5-7693ea3637b0\"><li local-id=\"c5fa6e0b-f941-4366-abb2-cc2762c4b938\"><p local-id=\"724bfdd7-38f8-4758-8649-6c2ca7e3e363\">Low-cost credit with flexible repayment options</p></li><li local-id=\"3e2069ab-c411-4a35-bc91-6426c3651314\"><p local-id=\"47db7f83-e507-45a1-9d1b-f8de56a4f792\">A clear value ladder with increasing benefits</p></li><li local-id=\"e856c031-832c-4632-96a5-a0b72c99e4d3\"><p local-id=\"a0e2e4af-8e2b-4e1f-83b2-a81590ddd2c5\">Behaviour-led rewards and loyalty mechanics</p></li><li local-id=\"c706609c-037c-4153-8353-0034d7b13a1b\"><p local-id=\"e9e5f70d-b919-4548-a4cd-3cb67a90b291\">Everyday savings and spend optimisation</p></li><li local-id=\"1cbc2d59-ecfa-49aa-afb0-96eb374dc88f\"><p local-id=\"55e7c904-d19e-47d3-b741-109e8b62b699\">Lifestyle partnerships and perks</p></li><li local-id=\"2f496d2c-e62a-4987-991d-e3fcf3b022d1\"><p local-id=\"0e2a07e7-7812-4afc-b643-2a1a6c966c5b\">Tools that provide visibility, control, and confidence</p></li><li local-id=\"aa291066-ee86-49d7-8088-0fb09fd8872d\"><p local-id=\"5907491b-9b3f-4faa-b3d8-a4ec0d8d4820\">Tiered experiences that reward engagement and progression</p></li></ul><p local-id=\"f1922bee-4bde-41bc-bcff-46b86bdae482\"><strong>What outcomes can we deliver for Zilch?</strong></p><ul local-id=\"6d16f76f-0b3c-4179-9007-ce059db62590\"><li local-id=\"7a7d24f4-d8ec-4e40-ab41-14a802f7e914\"><p local-id=\"618b8cd1-51a5-45ea-b6b3-65327a2608bb\">Increased paid membership penetration</p></li><li local-id=\"4cb12ce3-e7c3-4e53-9b0b-06044474a900\"><p local-id=\"ae75469a-9254-4380-979c-5eb89f61f574\">Higher ARPU and recurring revenue</p></li><li local-id=\"9e8c0916-151b-4c89-9965-a6701627d5ef\"><p local-id=\"39f3244a-5e45-49e6-a80d-4814185422e5\">Improved GP margin through more sustainable rewards economics</p></li><li local-id=\"f515dfdc-7b5d-440f-8617-63cef147f2ae\"><p local-id=\"0110f88a-29e9-4f61-9d36-ebea8ce26b7e\">Increased customer retention and lifetime value</p></li><li local-id=\"4ea1f1f8-ef43-47f0-bfb1-dcd8f527315a\"><p local-id=\"22d71e85-ccd3-4b3c-9c5b-1edf112615e5\">Greater share of wallet and primary-card behaviour</p></li><li local-id=\"ec7e2ee4-6a6b-4803-901e-71f50aef779f\"><p local-id=\"2d5b5d78-b55d-4d88-b586-087c7b5d6c06\">Higher credit utilisation with responsible usage</p></li><li local-id=\"400f24e2-712f-4cc9-b18c-8a9aa5c72161\"><p local-id=\"6b4fb780-4d39-4c8f-ac04-e934aa9b5fbf\">Stronger differentiation and brand loyalty</p></li><li local-id=\"db73b47f-a0c3-46e1-9b49-cbcc36687f4e\"><p local-id=\"402e98de-ba30-405f-b192-57b139481fdf\">More scalable, predictable growth driven by memberships</p></li></ul><h3 local-id=\"2d37237c-38d3-41d4-bbe1-a8394eeb6535\">Vision Purpose Pyramid</h3></ac:layout-cell></ac:layout-section><ac:layout-section ac:type=\"two_equal\" ac:breakout-mode=\"wide\" ac:breakout-width=\"760\" ac:local-id=\"9fb5f1cb-73bc-4f98-8862-1057f0452dc1\"><ac:layout-cell ac:local-id=\"cbd8d9c9-c488-423c-9875-60c0d278ec36\"><p local-id=\"895f810c-e389-4cad-9c0c-83be7fd25bbf\">Using the outputs from the workshop, we refined the findings into a clear purpose pyramid, with customers forming the foundation, the role of memberships at the core, and the intended business outcomes at the apex. </p><p local-id=\"967f7055-1624-4ad5-b995-dccf51d23a5b\">This structure was then used to define the memberships vision outlined below.</p></ac:layout-cell><ac:layout-cell ac:local-id=\"688a01f9-2413-4972-aa7c-0c0238b8ea06\"><ac:image ac:align=\"center\" ac:layout=\"center\" ac:original-height=\"385\" ac:original-width=\"503\" ac:custom-width=\"true\" ac:local-id=\"4d0d7c38-d80b-4449-87dd-578ff6111c8d\" ac:alt=\"image-20251214-160414.png\" ac:width=\"274\"><ri:attachment ri:filename=\"image-20251214-160414.png\" ri:version-at-save=\"1\" /><ac:caption ac:local-id=\"eeec6144-5382-4f71-b78c-58ce3bfdeb2e\"><p>Memberships Purpose</p></ac:caption></ac:image></ac:layout-cell></ac:layout-section><ac:layout-section ac:type=\"fixed-width\" ac:breakout-mode=\"default\"><ac:layout-cell><h3 local-id=\"7525f1cb-4584-4b90-98ba-c5bb6dd3e941\">Vision Statement</h3><p local-id=\"b0a63021-6879-47f0-b970-2ce4cd648e0d\">&ldquo;Empower customers to maximise the value they spend with Zilch through memberships that reward loyalty, enhance lifestyle and strengthen lasting, profitable, engagement.&rdquo;</p><h2 local-id=\"2864db13-8388-4ff2-94cc-01f5df930f9d\">Strategic Opportunities Outcomes</h2><p local-id=\"41d867db-084c-46c1-bf7c-657d61061bd0\">In the second phase of the workshop, we built on the insights generated during the vision-setting session to identify a long list of strategic opportunities for Zilch. These were then synthesised and refined into the key themes outlined below.</p><p local-id=\"02ab1dbf-0dc4-4160-b513-197f15d3d119\"><strong>Opportunity Themes</strong></p><ul local-id=\"04ea73ba-1990-45e2-9b56-4f04c848ccfb\"><li local-id=\"e43bad20-3b4f-4a36-9171-c5703917f782\"><p local-id=\"60c68ea9-cc32-4f00-b968-e39b229d03c3\">Cheaper tier below Plus</p></li><li local-id=\"d6a8ce67-bf26-4dd8-914c-242f96e06703\"><p local-id=\"8bc65a4e-bd42-4757-a997-50fad6b3f4a2\">Plus retention</p></li><li local-id=\"209eb413-8ba2-43d8-b25c-8e21a997de0f\"><p local-id=\"4e2b00b0-1001-4c9a-866b-26e557de8fa0\">Gamification mechanics</p></li><li local-id=\"37b93c27-7bdd-4134-9d0e-74fcac708d1d\"><p local-id=\"c20d94e8-a137-496a-b78d-123684a83ff7\">Prizes and one-off rewards</p></li><li local-id=\"d8367506-e799-4812-9a70-a1443b0d6aca\"><p local-id=\"ee95b604-77cc-4a1b-af58-1624bfee37df\">Improved rewards proposition</p></li><li local-id=\"d8433af8-dd06-46c6-bebd-06d3643e48d9\"><p local-id=\"997d26a5-3d6e-45ec-a6a3-4d2a6f2fef71\">Paid add-ons</p></li><li local-id=\"8c881358-c697-4058-b8a2-3ed62cd12d2e\"><p local-id=\"3d69bf13-0674-4a9c-9b94-d7024908c490\">Enhancing the existing membership proposition</p></li><li local-id=\"2bd819eb-7f7c-4e5b-a228-3d8b91c23b8d\"><p local-id=\"27cb09fc-96a4-49ef-afd9-eee61ad246e7\">Cancellation flow optimisation</p></li></ul><h3 local-id=\"b63e465b-59ed-420c-acf8-5e45be829d99\">Strategic Pillars of Memberships</h3></ac:layout-cell></ac:layout-section><ac:layout-section ac:type=\"two_equal\" ac:breakout-mode=\"wide\" ac:breakout-width=\"760\" ac:local-id=\"ccf3c0e1-a726-4331-a827-41d8313f6a4f\"><ac:layout-cell ac:local-id=\"03d90024-8e19-40b0-869c-7b5ec2a56bbe\"><p local-id=\"1a6ce500-8f00-4c1e-828e-abde34c3bc05\">We used these themes to define a set of strategic pillars that underpin and guide the evolution of our memberships proposition, ensuring that future initiatives remain aligned to our vision, customer needs, and long-term business objectives.</p></ac:layout-cell><ac:layout-cell ac:local-id=\"ec2fd480-8a6e-45cd-bfc3-825604b7c14a\"><ac:image ac:align=\"center\" ac:layout=\"center\" ac:original-height=\"159\" ac:original-width=\"510\" ac:custom-width=\"true\" ac:local-id=\"484b291a-8454-4b25-a023-9aaeda3bc665\" ac:alt=\"image-20251214-161510.png\" ac:width=\"510\"><ri:attachment ri:filename=\"image-20251214-161510.png\" ri:version-at-save=\"1\" /><ac:caption ac:local-id=\"5e8096fa-ea1c-49d4-a36d-81a5d2cbb41b\"><p>Memberships Strategic Pillars</p></ac:caption></ac:image></ac:layout-cell></ac:layout-section><ac:layout-section ac:type=\"fixed-width\" ac:breakout-mode=\"default\"><ac:layout-cell><h2 local-id=\"62a0c075-0975-45b0-9dd2-05ddd9fdf631\"><strong>Where the Current Strategy Falls Short</strong></h2><h3 local-id=\"3d9378af-1211-48e9-898b-a34f512bcba0\">Tier Structure</h3><p local-id=\"d4504571-fc38-40a9-bad2-954819fac8cb\">While the early performance of Plus demonstrates clear customer appetite for a paid membership proposition, the current tier structure limits broader adoption to achieve our revised goal. Zilch&rsquo;s customer base is uniquely price-sensitive compared to many competitors, reflecting the needs and behaviours of the segments we serve. As a result, the &pound;3.99 price point may be too high, and the proposition too rich, for a large proportion of customers who are willing to pay but do not fully realise value from the tangible rewards offered. At the other end of the spectrum, a higher-priced premium offering such as Zilch Ultimate is likely to have weaker product&ndash;market fit with our customer base and is therefore unlikely to achieve meaningful penetration at this stage of scaling our proposition. Together, this leaves a gap in the tier structure between Standard and Plus, constraining our ability to scale paid membership adoption.</p><h3 local-id=\"9211d15e-a14d-43e9-b305-71da329f489d\">Rewards Economics Challenge</h3><p local-id=\"013f90f2-2c28-4347-a2ca-15f10b99c2e9\">The current Rewards model scales linearly with customer spend, meaning that as customers become more engaged and progress up the membership value ladder, reward costs increase disproportionately and begin to negatively impact margins. In effect, higher engagement directly translates to higher cost, with limited levers available to control or optimise margin. The existing mechanics also do not sufficiently incentivise profitable behaviours, making it difficult to reward engagement in a way that aligns with business outcomes. As a result, introducing new or richer reward mechanics typically requires additional subsidy, limiting our ability to increase value for customers as they move up the membership tiers.</p><p local-id=\"bd6426e5-e9b5-4129-be8d-853561cdbaab\">More here: <ac:link ac:anchor=\"Why-Change\"><ri:page ri:content-title=\"Zilch Points\" ri:version-at-save=\"22\" /><ac:link-body>Zilch Points</ac:link-body></ac:link> </p><h2 local-id=\"6aa16648-81f4-4117-a84a-041dfe588266\">Memberships Strategy</h2></ac:layout-cell></ac:layout-section><ac:layout-section ac:type=\"single\" ac:breakout-mode=\"wide\" ac:breakout-width=\"760\" ac:local-id=\"38124dae-9b7e-4b7a-980d-72d145350c54\"><ac:layout-cell ac:local-id=\"552eb407-7e59-4377-a7b0-86264858b433\"><ac:image ac:align=\"center\" ac:layout=\"center\" ac:original-height=\"637\" ac:original-width=\"531\" ac:custom-width=\"true\" ac:local-id=\"0e91a92b-4391-4e70-8c75-8b93c7fb8bf2\" ac:alt=\"image-20251214-164516.png\" ac:width=\"531\"><ri:attachment ri:filename=\"image-20251214-164516.png\" ri:version-at-save=\"1\" /><ac:caption ac:local-id=\"b6c6440a-80e7-43c9-b4a4-9630cc5b91b8\"><p>Memberships Strategy</p></ac:caption></ac:image><p local-id=\"46fce293-6ce8-4039-93e0-5243bb534630\">This strategy sets out how memberships can evolve into an even stronger lever for growth and profitability at Zilch, informed by early learnings from Zilch Plus in market, a deep understanding of our customers, and insights generated through the cross-functional strategy workshop. Grounded in the role memberships play in customers&rsquo; everyday financial lives, the strategy focuses on delivering increasing value as engagement deepens - elevating everyday value, enhancing lifestyle, rewarding meaningful behaviours, and giving customers greater control and confidence over their money. Together, these pillars create a clear, scalable framework to drive stronger retention, accelerate membership adoption, deepen engagement, and align customer value with long-term, sustainable business outcomes.</p><h2 local-id=\"eb715366-7b36-4db2-8b8e-a33428c33640\">Strategic Initiatives to Realise the Vision</h2><p local-id=\"ba403a70-a6ba-452d-a030-115e3608b61b\">Guided by the memberships vision and strategic pillars, and informed by the opportunities identified through the workshop, this sequence of delivery is designed to maximise membership penetration and ensure the strategy is delivered effectively and efficiently.</p><h3 local-id=\"eb96db85-1d75-4a92-bf31-bcccfa63ebcd\">Zilch Pro</h3><p local-id=\"ea9b5795-26af-4813-aa18-fd954eee3c81\">Zilch Pro remains a critical component of the memberships strategy and we should stay the course with its launch and evolution. Pro enables us to achieve our long-term growth and profitability objectives by providing a platform to introduce richer, more differentiated tiers over time. It creates a clear sense of aspiration and exclusivity for customers to work towards, helping to reward our most engaged users while strengthening emotional loyalty. Importantly, Pro also plays a key commercial role by retaining our highest-value customers, encouraging primary spend behaviour, and improving GP by migrating highly engaged Plus members into a higher-value tier.</p><h3 local-id=\"36f17cbb-1cb8-4ec3-91db-b19d3a4c9118\">Zilch Points</h3><p local-id=\"f7647eea-8b2d-4eb3-a6b6-f62ad25b6af0\">Rather than introducing an additional membership tier beyond Pro, the next phase of investment should focus on reworking the Rewards proposition at Zilch. With the launch of Pro, we will have established a strong and coherent membership value ladder, offering clear progression from free through to premium and giving customers natural points of aspiration as their engagement deepens. This ladder provides a stable foundation that we can continue to leverage and optimise, allowing us to focus on evolving Rewards as a core system that underpins the entire memberships ecosystem, rather than adding further structural complexity.</p><p local-id=\"87d1f9b2-7c90-444a-b64f-be7f9d38c3f6\">Reworking Rewards into Zilch Points enables us to move away from a linear, cashback-led model towards a more scalable and economically sustainable approach. Points give us far greater control over cost while unlocking more sophisticated incentive mechanics, allowing us to reward higher-margin and strategically important behaviours more strongly. </p><p local-id=\"96a90a31-2236-43fc-85b9-7b628dfbd1d5\">While this will result in a weaker base offering over time, customers on higher membership tiers will ultimately be better off than those outside of the memberships proposition, creating a clear and fair progression path. Points also introduce a flywheel effect: as customers engage more, they earn more value, which in turn drives deeper engagement and progression up the ladder. </p><p local-id=\"0be35fa9-653e-4478-8339-a18683c7789f\">Importantly, the goal is not to weaken Rewards overall, but to make them more cost-effective for the business while ensuring that customers who take high-value actions receive greater value than they do today. To succeed, we must ensure Zilch Points deliver genuine, tangible value, as Rewards remain a core part of Zilch&rsquo;s proposition and over-correcting could risk disengagement or churn.</p><h3 local-id=\"7c6d1fd7-9e9f-4a51-a3fe-8a0911423e20\">Zilch Extra</h3><p local-id=\"6c0978c1-ae84-442b-b72f-d111e09d1b13\">Introducing a new paid tier Zilch Extra, would create a more accessible entry point into memberships and unlock broader paid adoption. Priced at around &pound;1.99, Extra would be positioned as a stripped-back version of Zilch Plus, offering a focused set of core benefits rather than a fully-featured proposition. This would include essential perks such as priority support, tastecard, and access to Zilch Points at a lower earn rate than Plus, aligned to the new points model. To further enhance perceived value, Extra could also include a credit insights feature, available across all paid tiers while remaining excluded from Standard. By limiting benefits such as a free physical card or spending Rewards (or points) anywhere, Zilch Extra remains clearly differentiated from Plus, while providing a compelling, low-friction step up from the free tier.</p><h3 local-id=\"c1f2a2d5-50e2-46dd-8e31-84772da12098\">Zilch Ultimate</h3></ac:layout-cell></ac:layout-section><ac:layout-section ac:type=\"fixed-width\" ac:breakout-mode=\"default\"><ac:layout-cell><p local-id=\"3597c3bd-4fbf-4442-a34d-ef9b9d27a1e9\">Once a mature and scalable memberships structure is in place, there may be an opportunity to introduce Zilch Ultimate as a future, top-tier offering. Ultimate would be designed for power users who want a fully comprehensive experience, with Zilch taking care of as much of their financial and lifestyle needs as possible. Priced at around &pound;16.99, the tier would bundle the highest levels of value, protection, exclusivity, and recognition into a single membership, leveraging the most powerful capabilities of Zilch&rsquo;s ad-subsidised payments ecosystem. Ultimate would be positioned for customers who choose to place Zilch at the centre of their everyday lives, offering a premium, all-in proposition for the most engaged segment of the customer base.</p><p local-id=\"c65d0d9d-4eba-424a-bbb8-6762403b745f\" /></ac:layout-cell></ac:layout-section></ac:layout>"}}

It covers customer migrations across tiers, cancellation/downgrade/upgrade logic, free trial handling, and payment transitions during subscription changes.</p><p local-id=\"8ba8809feb4a\">Also, it was created post-implementation, so it&rsquo;s reflecting how subscriptions really work.</p></ac:adf-content></ac:adf-node><ac:adf-fallback><div class=\"panel conf-macro output-block\" style=\"background-color: rgb(234,230,255);border-color: rgb(153,141,217);border-width: 1.0px;\"><div class=\"panelContent\" style=\"background-color: rgb(234,230,255);\">\n<p local-id=\"490f3daa0d55\">This document consolidates the technical design, focusing on product-tier-based subscriptions. It covers customer migrations across tiers, cancellation/downgrade/upgrade logic, free trial handling, and payment transitions during subscription changes.</p><p local-id=\"8ba8809feb4a\">Also, it was created post-implementation, so it&rsquo;s reflecting how subscriptions really work.</p>\n</div></div></ac:adf-fallback></ac:adf-extension><p local-id=\"153186ae86ce\" /><p architecture design:</p><ul local-id=\"1ddfe705e03a\"><li local-id=\"4ad9f0cb36b3\"><p local-id=\"0a8be44fda31\"><a href=\"https://payzilch.atlassian.net/wiki/x/SoDFAgE\" local-id=\"4fc1a2661fc1\" data-card-appearance=\"inline\">https://payzilch.atlassian.net/wiki/x/SoDFAgE</a> </p></li><li local-id=\"90176322b5ff\"><p local-id=\"7343c10e744c\"><a href=\"https://payzilch.stoplight.io/docs/product-api/branches/simplified%20version/769d57131c3f0-product-service-database-schema\">https://payzilch.stoplight.io/docs/product-api/branches/simplified local-id=\"b50af2cd3746\"><p local-id=\"8e3a8b4a5d8c\">Product docs:<a href=\"https://payzilch.atlassian.net/wiki/x/GABr-/\" local-id=\"e3fcf7ecce45\" data-card-appearance=\"inline\">https://payzilch.atlassian.net/wiki/x/GABr-/</a> </p></li></ul><p local-id=\"c977fdb14a99\" /><h2 local-id=\"8fd09abac4d2\">Architecture Overview</h2><p local-id=\"41c9534112c7\">Subscriptions are owned by the Product Service. It manages subscription lifecycle, emits domain events, and coordinates with Payments for billing/charges and with Customer for product alignment.</p><h2 local-id=\"a8c76081a4fa\">State Model and Lifecycle</h2><p local-id=\"e73b9cc06ac0\">Each subscription instance progresses through states that reflect entitlement and billing status.</p><h3 local-id=\"6e2a3cf368e2\">States</h3><ul local-id=\"f6faa2432408\"><li local-id=\"3480f492536b\"><p local-id=\"96c4955effd3\"><code>PENDING_START</code>: Not an active state. Billing scheduled. Awaiting the first payment, which should activate the subscription.</p></li><li local-id=\"7b28cfacbce9\"><p local-id=\"c3242ca4ca3f\"><code>STARTED</code>: Active subscription, could be in trial period/after trial/without trial. Billing is scheduled.</p></li><li local-id=\"b1668b3a5370\"><p local-id=\"cf37c71d7832\"><code>PENDING_CANCELLATION</code>: Still active subscription. Billing cancelled. Will transition to CANCELLED on the end date.</p></li><li local-id=\"48c0548709b2\"><p local-id=\"ce302a1505e3\"><code>PAYMENT_FAILED</code>: Active subscription. Payment failed, but the grace period is open (3 days). Billing retries scheduled.</p></li><li local-id=\"06b33410187d\"><p local-id=\"0df8efb9018e\"><code>PENDING_DOWNGRADE</code>: Active subscription. Downgrade requested by a customer. Transition to lower tier scheduled for next billing date.</p></li><li local-id=\"196f05c92417\"><p local-id=\"1ec85ab9ebca\"><code>CANCELLED</code>: Terminated; no renewal;</p></li></ul><h2 local-id=\"c944e556ae61\">Migration Scenarios Between Tiers</h2><ac:structured-macro ac:name=\"info\" ac:schema-version=\"1\" ac:local-id=\"3b4d1ca4afad\" ac:macro-id=\"047acf01-151e-42e4-90cf-47ea2b8f68ed\"><ac:rich-text-body><p local-id=\"042cffafcb56\">Currently, we support 3 product tiers: </p><ul local-id=\"53e83fb9e868\"><li local-id=\"408875ffd670\"><p local-id=\"c2a1b8382969\">FREE - sample product: zilch-up-standard</p></li><li local-id=\"9c727a8e45e6\"><p local-id=\"48c0a461ff20\">PLUS - sample product: zilch-up-plus</p></li><li local-id=\"101d63ed9a98\"><p local-id=\"e7c550ff544e\">PRO - sample product: zilch-up-pro</p></li></ul></ac:rich-text-body></ac:structured-macro><p local-id=\"97ae8206f2b8\">The diagrams below describe how a customer moves between <strong>FREE</strong>, <strong>PLUS</strong> and <strong>PRO</strong> tiers.</p><ul local-id=\"8fe15bd3-3aa7-4113-885f-890e47534b15\"><li local-id=\"1529d210-7583-495e-a1cc-db35b3a4e375\"><p local-id=\"1a7a70b1602a\"><strong>Single active subscription</strong> at any time (FREE is represented by &ldquo;no active subscription&rdquo;).</p></li><li local-id=\"73986609-16e5-448d-b2d3-4951b1cc8c47\"><p local-id=\"2c22ce950050\"><strong>Global free trial</strong>: at most one free trial across all tiers (Plus/Pro).</p></li></ul><hr local-id=\"75f73714-4627-478f-8e61-962e58f08e66\" /><h3 local-id=\"85579ce4d62a\">1. Subscription lifecycle diagram</h3><ac:structured-macro ac:name=\"mermaid\" ac:schema-version=\"1\" data-layout=\"default\" ac:local-id=\"37991846-36de-4b12-947d-a6cc16768459\" ac:macro-id=\"881a954f-e2dc-48a9-b191-a34e43260217\"><ac:parameter ac:name=\"size\">xl</ac:parameter><ac:parameter ac:name=\"isEditable\">true</ac:parameter><ac:parameter ac:name=\"diagramCode\">flowchart TD\n    FREE[&quot;FREE tier&lt;br/&gt;(no active subscription)&quot;]\n    PS[&quot;PENDING_START &quot;]\n    ST[&quot;STARTED&quot;]\n    PD[&quot;PENDING_DOWNGRADE&quot;]\n    PF[&quot;PAYMENT_FAILED&lt;br/&gt;(3â€‘day grace period)&quot;]\n    PC[&quot;PENDING_CANCELLATION (no longer billed)&quot;]\n    CA[&quot;CANCELLED &quot;]\n    %% Activation\n    FREE --&gt; ST\n    PS --&gt; |&quot;Start planned after downgrade&quot;| ST\n    %% Upgrade / downgrade between paid tiers\n    ST --&gt;|&quot;Upgrade&lt;br/&gt;(Immediate)&quot;| CA\n    ST --&gt;|&quot;Downgrade&lt;br/&gt;(Effective at period end. # Detailed Summary: Everything About Zilch Pro in Confluence

## Executive Summary

**Zilch Pro** is Zilch's premium-tier paid membership offering, positioned above Zilch Plus, priced at **Â£7.99 per month**. It builds on the success of Zilch Plus (Â£3.99/month) and is targeted at Zilch's most highly engaged customers. The product is planned for launch in **March 2026**, with staff testing beginning in mid-February 2026.

---

| Physical Card | Â£4.99 | Free | Free Pro card |
| Customer Service | Standard | Priority | **24/7 Premier Support** |
| Tastecard Membership | âŒ | âœ… | âœ… |

## 3. Experimentation Plan

### **Approach**
Two parallel cohorts will be run to gather insights:

1. **MAU Cohort** â€“ Lifecycle and penetration learning (adoption, retention, benefit usage)
2. **Plus MAU Cohort (10k)** â€“ Statistically powered measurement of financial impact (GMV/GP per user)

### **Key Questions**
- **Lifecycle:** Will top 20-30% of Plus customers adopt Pro? How many non-Plus adopters will subscribe to Pro? Will Pro users retain at the same rate as Plus? Are they using Pro benefits?
- **Financial:** Will Pro users change their spend? Will they become more profitable than Plus users?

### **Key Metrics**
- GP per User
- Penetration (Plus MAUs, PMF MAUs, Total MAUs)
- GMV per User
- Adoption and Retention rates
- Credit/Debit split
- Benefit utilisation

### **Power Analysis Findings**
With a 10k sample size at 25% adoption, a **+12% GMV lift** amongst Pro adopters can be detected (presenting as +3% lift in treatment vs control).

### **Learnings from Plus Launch**
- Avoid 1% LaunchDarkly rollouts â€“ assign customers explicitly from a defined list
- Ensure treatment and control groups are statistically identical before launch
- Enforce consistent naming conventions
- Inform stakeholders proactively when cohorts go live
- Ensure rewards logic is built into the PnL

**ðŸ“„ Reference:** [Zilch Pro Experimentation Plan](https://payzilch.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/ZP/pages/4949016869/Zilch+Pro+Experimentation+Plan)

---

## 4. Marketing & Communications

### **Customer Scenarios**

#### **Upgrades (Instant)**
| Scenario | Details |
|----------|---------|
| Standard â†’ Pro | Instant upgrade, first charge today |
| Standard â†’ Pro (free trial) | 1 month free trial, first charge in +1 month |
| Plus â†’ Pro | Remaining Plus days converted to Pro days at pro-rata rate |
| Plus (free trial) â†’ Pro | Remaining free trial days converted |

#### **Downgrades (Scheduled for next billing cycle)**
| Scenario | Details |
|----------|---------|
| Pro â†’ Plus | Customer remains on Pro until next billing date |
| Pro â†’ Standard | Customer remains on Pro until next billing date |

### **Communications Required**
- **Subscription upgrade email** (Plus â†’ Pro)
- **Resume subscription email** (for pending cancellation)
- **Push notifications** for various scenarios
- **In-app explainers** for upgrade/downgrade flows

### **Go-Live Dates**
- Staff: 2 February 2026
- Customers: 2 March 2026

## 5. Memberships Strategy

### **Vision Statement**
> *"Empower customers to maximise the value they spend with Zilch through memberships that reward loyalty, enhance lifestyle and strengthen lasting, profitable, engagement."*

### **Strategic Pillars**
1. Elevate everyday value
2. Enhance lifestyle
3. Reward meaningful behaviours
4. Give customers greater control and confidence over their money

### **Pro's Strategic Role**
- Provides a platform to introduce richer, more differentiated tiers over time
- Creates aspiration and exclusivity for customers
- Retains highest-value customers
- Encourages primary spend behaviour
- Improves GP by migrating highly engaged Plus users to a higher-value tier
- Creates a "value anchor" that enhances perceived value of Plus

### **Future Roadmap**
- **Zilch Points** â€“ Rework Rewards into a scalable points-based model
- **Zilch Extra** â€“ New Â£1.99 tier below Plus as accessible entry point
- **Zilch Ultimate** â€“ Future top-tier at ~Â£16.99 for power users

**ðŸ“„ Reference:** [Memberships Strategy](https://payzilch.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/ZP/pages/4899143704/Memberships+Strategy)

---

## 6. Technical Implementation

### **Architecture**
- Subscriptions are managed by the **Product Service**
- Coordinates with **Payments** for billing/charges
- Coordinates with **Customer** for product alignment

### **Subscription States**
| State | Description |
|-------|-------------|
| `PENDING_START` | Billing scheduled, awaiting first payment |
| `STARTED` | Active subscription (trial/post-trial) |
| `PENDING_CANCELLATION` | Active but billing cancelled, will cancel at end date |
| `PAYMENT_FAILED` | Active, 3-day grace period, retries scheduled |
| `PENDING_DOWNGRADE` | Active, downgrade scheduled for next billing date |
| `CANCELLED` | Terminated, no renewal |

### **Product Tiers Supported**
- **FREE** â€“ e.g., `zilch-up-standard`
- **PLUS** â€“ e.g., `zilch-up-plus`
- **PRO** â€“ e.g., `zilch-up-pro`

### **Migration Rules**
- **Single active subscription** at any time
- **Global free trial**: At most one free trial across all tiers (Plus/Pro)
- Upgrades: Immediate
- Downgrades: Scheduled for next billing date

**ðŸ“„ Reference:** [Technical Design: Subscriptions and Migration Between Product Tiers](https://payzilch.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/PAYZ/pages/5050040321/Technical+Design+Subscriptions+and+Migration+Between+Product+Tiers)

## 7. Pivot Strategy (February 2026)

### **Current Status (Iteration 11)**

#### **Zilch Plus Optimisations**
| Item | Status |
|------|--------|
| Memberships in onboarding flow | âœ… Complete |
| Resume cancelled membership | âœ… Complete |
| No Credit rewards on late instalments | ðŸŸ¡ In Progress |
| Discounted memberships | ðŸŸ¡ In Progress |
| Membership cancellation card charge | ðŸ”´ Not Started |
| Extending free trials | ðŸ”´ Not Started |
| Pending rewards | ðŸ”´ Not Started |

#### **Zilch Pro Benefits**
| Item | Status |
|------|--------|
| Customer service (Premier Support) | âœ… Complete |
| Higher Rewards | âœ… Complete |
| Physical Card | ðŸŸ¡ In Progress |
| Free Snooze | ðŸ”´ Not Started |
| Partnerships | ðŸ”´ Not Started |

### **Strategic Pivot Options**
Multiple strategies under consideration with various resourcing levels:
- **Existing resourcing**: Deliver original plan, launch Pro in ~6 months
- **Reduced resourcing (Rewards-led)**: Launch Pro MVP early with higher reward rates
- **Reduced resourcing (Partner-led)**: Complete partner integrations before launch
- **Path 1 (Increased resourcing)**: Deliver memberships North Star
- **Path 1.5**: Improve memberships and paywall Standard features
- **Path 2**: Alter core business model with aggressive paywalling

**ðŸ“„ Reference:** [Zilch Memberships Pivot Strategy](https://payzilch.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/ZP/pages/5073961037/Zilch+Memberships+Pivot+Strategy)

## Summary

Zilch Pro represents a significant evolution in Zilch's membership strategy, offering premium benefits to highly engaged customers at Â£7.99/month. With a planned launch in March 2026, the product is designed to:

1. **Increase ARPU** through a higher subscription tier
2. **Improve customer retention** by offering exclusive benefits
3. **Strengthen GP margins** by migrating high-engagement Plus users
4. **Create a clear value ladder** from Standard â†’ Plus â†’ Pro

The project involves cross-functional coordination across Product, Engineering, Design, Marketing, Customer Service, and Compliance teams, with comprehensive planning documented across the various Confluence spaces.
